The traditional <em>IP</em> Address (known as IPv4) uses a 32-bit number to represent an <em>IP</em> address, and it defines both network and host address. A 32-bit number is capable of providing roughly 4 billion unique numbers, and hence IPv4 addresses running out as more devices are connected to the <em>IP</em> network.</span></div></div></div></div><!--n--></div><div class="g"><!--m--><div data-hveid="65" data-ved="0ahUKEwjtha76j-zUAhUGaT4KHVCCA3UQFQhBKAMwBA"><div class="rc"><h3 class="r"><a href="https://www.iplocation.net/hide-ip-with-vpn" onmousedown="return rwt(this,'','','','5','AFQjCNFHgw6qqFeyhMIsUSXmzvo9Si8PqA','','0ahUKEwjtha76j-zUAhUGaT4KHVCCA3UQFghCMAQ','','',event)">How to hide your IP Address with VPN? - IP Location</a></h3><div class="s"><div><div class="f kv _SWb" style="white-space:nowrap"><cite class="_Rm">https://www.iplocation.net/hide-ip-with-vpn</cite><div class="action-menu ab_ctl"><a class="_Fmb ab_button" href="#" id="am-b4" aria-label="Result details" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="true" role="button" jsaction="m.tdd;keydown:m.hbke;keypress:m.mskpe" data-ved="0ahUKEwjtha76j-zUAhUGaT4KHVCCA3UQ7B0IQzAE"><span class="mn-dwn-arw"></span></a><div class="action-menu-panel ab_dropdown" role="menu" tabindex="-1" jsaction="keydown:m.hdke;mouseover:m.hdhne;mouseout:m.hdhue" data-ved="0ahUKEwjtha76j-zUAhUGaT4KHVCCA3UQqR8IRDAE"><ol><li class="action-menu-item ab_dropdownitem" role="menuitem"><a class="fl" href="https://webcache.googleusercontent.com/search?q=cache:FNVi8z3rFk8J:https://www.iplocation.net/hide-ip-with-vpn+&amp;cd=5&amp;hl=en&amp;ct=clnk&amp;gl=us" onmousedown="return rwt(this,'','','','5','AFQjCNEdr5wAXkBiSoSXUhgVmaXYy9MoPw','','0ahUKEwjtha76j-zUAhUGaT4KHVCCA3UQIAhFMAQ','','',event)">Cached</a></li></ol></div></div></div><span class="st">Hide your geolocation of your <em>IP</em> address by obtaining a new <em>IP</em> address from a VPN ...
